setup_backward_industry = {
	set_variable = { RUS_prev_month_num_of_factories = ROOT.num_of_factories }
	add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_backward_industry_modifier }
	add_ideas = rus_industry_lack
	recalculate_backward_industry_debuff = yes
}
remove_backward_industry = {
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_backward_industry_modifier }
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_industrialized_nation_modifier }		
	}
	swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = rus_industry_lack
		add_idea = rus_industrialised_nation
	}
}
setup_unfinished_land_reform = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				state = 217
				state = 250
				state = 251
				state = 249
				state = 252
				state = 219
				state = 195
				state = 652
				state = 651
				state = 572
				state = 572
				state = 653
				state = 571
				state = 570
				state = 40
				state = 568
				state = 566
				state = 399
				state = 399
			}
		}
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_unfinished_land_reform_modifier	} 
	}
	add_ideas = rus_unfinished_land_reform
}
destroy_unfinished_land_reform = {
	remove_ideas = rus_unfinished_land_reform
	set_global_flag = RUS_land_reform_finished
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_unfinished_land_reform_modifier }
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_unfinished_land_reform_modifier	} 
		}		
	}
}
recalculate_monthly_industrialisation_rate = {
	
	set_variable = { RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate = ROOT.num_of_factories }
	subtract_from_variable = { RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate = RUS_prev_month_num_of_factories }
	divide_variable = { RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate = ROOT.num_of_factories }
	divide_variable = { RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate = 100 }
	set_variable = { RUS_prev_month_num_of_factories = ROOT.num_of_factories }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_idea = rus_industry_lack }
		}
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_efficiency_gain = 0.05 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_max_efficiency = 0.05 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_industrial_capacity = 0.1 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_production_speed_buildings = 0.05 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_research_speed = 0.03 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_political_power_gain = 0.05 }
		
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_efficiency_gain = RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_max_efficiency = RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_industrial_capacity = RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_production_speed_buildings = RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_research_speed = RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate }
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_political_power_gain = RUS_backward_industry_industrialisation_rate }
	}
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
}

recalculate_backward_industry_debuff = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_factories < 220
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_var = ROOT.num_of_factories }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = RUS_industrialisation_var
			min = 50
			max = 220
		}
		divide_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_var = 220 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = RUS_industrialisation_var
			min = 0
			max = 1
		}
		set_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_2_var = RUS_industrialisation_var }
		set_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_3_var = RUS_industrialisation_var }
		set_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_4_var = RUS_industrialisation_var }
		
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_factor = -1 }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_3_factor = -0.6 }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_4_factor = -0.55 }
		
		add_to_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_factor }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_2_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_factor }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_3_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_3_factor }
		add_to_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_4_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_4_factor }
		
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_var = -0.1 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_var }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_2_var = -0.14 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_2_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_2_var }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_3_var = -0.08 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_3_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_3_var }
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_negative_4_var = -0.8 }
		multiply_variable = { RUS_industrialisation_4_var = RUS_industrialisation_negative_4_var }
		
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_efficiency_gain = -0.7 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_max_efficiency = -0.7 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_industrial_capacity = -1 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_production_speed_buildings = -1 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_research_speed = -1.9 }
		set_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_political_power_gain = -1.3 }
	
		multiply_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_efficiency_gain = RUS_industrialisation_var }
		multiply_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_max_efficiency = RUS_industrialisation_var }
		multiply_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_industrial_capacity = RUS_industrialisation_2_var }
		multiply_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_production_speed_buildings = RUS_industrialisation_2_var }
		multiply_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_research_speed = RUS_industrialisation_3_var }
		multiply_variable = { ROOT.RUS_backward_industry_political_power_gain = RUS_industrialisation_4_var }
		
		clear_variable = RUS_industrialisation_var
		clear_variable = RUS_industrialisation_2_var
		clear_variable = RUS_industrialisation_3_var
		clear_variable = RUS_industrialisation_4_var
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	}
}
RUS_recheck_president_subideology = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			nsp_in_power = yes
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = bukharinist_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = bukharinist_subtype
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			plsr_in_power = yes
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = anarcho_syndicalist_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = anarcho_syndicalist_subtype
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Rafail_Abramovich_hog_sde
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Irakliy_G_Tsereteli_hog_sde
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = social_democrat_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = social_democrat_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_D_Nabokov_hog_mli
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = liberal_conservative_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = liberal_conservative_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Aleksandr_I_Konovalov_hog_mli
			has_government = market_liberal
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = market_liberal_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Viktor_M_Baydalakov_hog_npo
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = solidarism_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = solidarism_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_Felix_F_Yusupov_hog_ade
				has_idea = RUS_Georgiy_P_Ignatiev_hog_sco
				has_idea = RUS_Vasiliy_V_Shulgin_hog_sco
			}
			has_country_flag = RUS_DPROM
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Felix Yusupov"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = clientelism_subtype }
				}
				set_country_leader_ideology = clientelism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Pyotr Wrangel"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = soccon_bonapartism_subtype }
				}
				set_country_leader_ideology = soccon_bonapartism_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = moderate_authoritarianism_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = moderate_authoritarianism_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_M_Zenzinov_hog_sde
				has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_K_Volsky_hog_rso
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = socdem_narodism_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = socdem_narodism_subtype 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_M_Zenzinov_hog_sde
				has_idea = RUS_Vladimir_K_Volsky_hog_rso
			}
			has_country_flag = RUS_socdems_rpr
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader_ideology = socdem_left_nationalism_subtype }
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = socdem_left_nationalism_subtype 
		}
	}	
}

		rus_divided_staff2

	}

RUS_remove_riga_accords = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords }
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_1 }
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords_1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_2 }
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords_2
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_3 }
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords_3
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_4 }
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords_4
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_5 }
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords_5
	}
}
RUS_reduce_german_influence = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_5 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_german_influence_is_shrinking
		remove_ideas = rus_riga_accords_5
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_4 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_german_influence_is_shrinking
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_riga_accords_4
			add_idea = rus_riga_accords_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_3 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_german_influence_is_shrinking
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_riga_accords_3
			add_idea = rus_riga_accords_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_german_influence_is_shrinking
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_riga_accords_2
			add_idea = rus_riga_accords_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords_1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_german_influence_is_shrinking
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_riga_accords_1
			add_idea = rus_riga_accords_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_riga_accords }
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_german_influence_is_shrinking
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_riga_accords
			add_idea = rus_riga_accords_1
		}
	}
}
RUS_reduce_army_debuff = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_divided_staff6 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_divided_staff6
			add_idea = rus_experienced_military
		}
		clr_country_flag = rus_divided_army
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_divided_staff4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_divided_staff4
			add_idea = rus_divided_staff6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_divided_staff3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_divided_staff3
			add_idea = rus_divided_staff4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_divided_staff2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_divided_staff2
			add_idea = rus_divided_staff3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_divided_staff1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_divided_staff1
			add_idea = rus_divided_staff2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = rus_divided_staff }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_divided_staff
			add_idea = rus_divided_staff1
		}
	}
}
RUS_investment_increase = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = rus_investments3 }
				remove_ideas = rus_investments3
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = 	rus_investments4
				days = 365
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = rus_investments2 }
			remove_ideas = rus_investments2
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = 	rus_investments3
				days = 365
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = rus_investments1 }
			remove_ideas = rus_investments1
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = rus_investments2
				days = 365
				
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = rus_investments }
			remove_ideas = rus_investments
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = rus_investments1
				days = 365
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = {
				has_idea = rus_investments }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = rus_investments
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
}

		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_denikin_1
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_denikin_2
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_denikin_3
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_denikin_4
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_denikin_5
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_wrangel
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_wrangel_1
		remove_ideas = rus_junta_focus_wrangel_2
		remove_ideas = rus_loyal_military
	}
}
	
RUS_savinkov_power = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_russia_1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = RUS_new_russia_1
			add_idea = RUS_new_russia_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_russia_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = RUS_new_russia_2
			add_idea = RUS_new_russia_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_russia_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = RUS_new_russia_3
			add_idea = RUS_new_russia_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_russia_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = RUS_new_russia_4
			add_idea = RUS_new_russia_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_russia_5 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = RUS_new_russia_5
			add_idea = RUS_new_russia_6
		}
	}
}
RUS_setup_monarch_variables = {
	set_variable = { popular_support_monarchy = RUS_monarchy_popular_support }
	set_variable = { workers_support_monarchy = 0.1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_state_religion
		}
		set_variable = { clergy_support_monarchy = 0.8 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { clergy_support_monarchy = 0.6 }
	}
	set_variable = { bourgeois_support_monarchy = 0.5 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_DMI
				has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_PAVEL
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = { add_to_variable = { bourgeois_support_monarchy = 0.1 } }
			20 = { add_to_variable = { bourgeois_support_monarchy = 0.12 } }
			20 = { add_to_variable = { bourgeois_support_monarchy = 0.15 } }
			20 = { add_to_variable = { bourgeois_support_monarchy = 0.17 } }
			20 = { add_to_variable = { bourgeois_support_monarchy = 0.19 } }
		}
	}
	set_variable = { army_support_monarchy = army_support }
	random_list = {
		20 = { multiply_variable = { army_support_monarchy = 0.8 } }
		20 = { multiply_variable = { army_support_monarchy = 1.1 } }
		20 = { multiply_variable = { army_support_monarchy = 1.15 } }
		20 = { multiply_variable = { army_support_monarchy = 1.2 } }
		20 = { multiply_variable = { army_support_monarchy = 1.7 } }
	}
}
RUS_setup_russian_monarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_VLA
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_vladimir = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_DMI
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_dmitriy = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_PAVEL
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_pavel = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_ANA
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_anastasia = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_VRA_TSAR
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_wrangel_const = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_VSEV
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_vsevolod = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_ROMAN
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_roman = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_BORIS
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_boris = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_MIKH
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_mikhail = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_AND
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_andrei = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_NIK
		}
		RUS_setup_tsar_nicholas = yes
	}
	else = { #Kirill is now vanilla choice kinda
		RUS_setup_tsar_kirill = yes
	}	
	RUS_recheck_president_subideology = yes
}

setup_soviets_civil_war = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 195 #Petrograd
					state = 208 #Luga
					state = 209 #Pskov
					state = 210 #Velikiye Luki
					state = 219 #Moscow
					state = 220 #Kursk
					state = 224 #Bryansk
					state = 236 #Astrakhan
					state = 239 #Saratov
					state = 240 #Belgorod
					state = 242 #Smolensk
					state = 243 #Roslavl
					state = 244 #Volkhov
					state = 246 #Rzhev
					state = 247 #Tver
					state = 250 #Simbisrk
					state = 252 #Nizhny Novgorod
					state = 253 #Vladimir
					state = 254 #Ryazan
					state = 255 #Penza
					state = 256 #Cheboksary
					state = 263 #Novgorod
					state = 755 #Vitebsk
					state = 880 #Dvinsk
				}
			}
			SOV = { add_state_core = PREV }
		}
		release = SOV
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Motostrelkovaya Diviziya" }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Tankovaya Diviziya" }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Gornostrelkovaya Diviziya" }
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			target = SOV
			size = army_support
			navy_ratio = 0
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
		}
		SOV = {
			set_major = yes
			transfer_technology_without_doctrines = yes
			transfer_navy = { target = RUS }
			add_ideas = SOV_chaotic_revolution
			country_lock_all_division_template = yes
			add_state_claim = 329 #Tuva
			RUS_transfer_russian_ideas = yes
			add_ideas = {
				SOV_nationalist_resistance
				SOV_monarchist_resistance
				SOV_democrat_resistance
			}
			set_country_flag = SOV_must_deal_with_opposition
			country_event = {
				id = bolsheviks.1
				days = 7
			}
		}
		219 = { #Moscow
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Tankovaya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
				owner = SOV
				prioritize_location = 6380
				count = 3
			}
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Motostrelkovaya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
				owner = SOV
				prioritize_location = 6380
			}
		}
		217 = { #Tsarityn
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Gornostrelkovaya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 0.3"
				owner = SOV
				prioritize_location = 6380
				count = 4
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = SOV.owned_states
			remove_core_of = RUS
			add_claim_by = RUS
			teleport_armies = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = RUS.core_states
			add_core_of = SOV
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_claimed_by = RUS }
			add_claim_by = SOV
		}
		set_major = yes
		remove_ideas = RUS_army_mutiny
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 402 }	
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = hidden_sympathies
			}
			remove_unit_leader_trait = hidden_sympathies
			set_nationality = SOV
			SOV = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 455 }
					set_leader_portrait = GFX_Portrait_Soviet_Vasily_Chuikov
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 17897 }
					set_leader_portrait = GFX_Portrait_SOV_Semyon_Hitler
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 447 }
					set_leader_portrait = GFX_Portrait_SOV_Aleksandr_Yegorov
				}
				random_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_id = 449 }	
					set_leader_portrait = GFX_Portrait_RUS_Gregory_Zhukov_General
				}
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				popularity = 0
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			set_country_flag = RUS_kornilov_coup
			add_ideas = RUS_Lavr_G_Kornilov_hog_pau
			add_ideas = RUS_Aleksey_A_Ignatiev_for_pau
			add_ideas = RUS_Ivan_P_Romanovskiy_eco_pau
			add_ideas = RUS_Aleksandr_P_Balk_sec_pau 
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Lavr Kornilov"
				desc = "POLITICS_LAVR_KORNILOV_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Lavr_Kornilov.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = junta_subtype
				traits = {}
			}			
			add_stability = 0.4
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.3
			}			
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			clr_country_flag = RUS_REVOL
			clr_country_flag = RUS_SEN
			clr_country_flag = RUS_democarcy
			clr_country_flag = RUS_demonstrations
			clr_country_flag = RUS_Okhrannoye_Otdeleniye_locked
			set_country_flag = RUS_JUNTA
			remove_ideas = rus_memories_of_rev
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = rus_political_instability1}
				remove_ideas = rus_political_instability1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = rus_political_instability}
				remove_ideas = rus_political_instability
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = RUS
				reset_russian_leaders = yes
				add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.1
				}
				add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.1
				}
				add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.1
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rusd.50
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

					retire = yes
				}
			}
			RRF = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = RUS
				}
			}
			RUS = {
				copy_government_of_ROOT = yes
				remove_all_AI_templates = yes
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Krasnaya Gvardiya" }

					SOV_monarchist_resistance_1

				transfer_technology = yes
				unlock_national_focus = RUS_Balance_The_Budget
				set_country_flag = unlock_military
				if = {

				}
				transfer_technology = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_land_reform_finished }
					}

				}

					set_stability = 0.6
					set_war_support = 0.5
				}
				add_ideas = civilian_economy
				add_ideas = volunteer_only
				hidden_effect = {
					add_stability = -0.5
					add_war_support = -0.5
				}				
				clr_country_flag = RUS_SEN
				clr_country_flag = RUS_Okhrannoye_Otdeleniye_locked
				clr_country_flag = RUS_JUNTA
				set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_vozhdct
				set_country_flag = RUS_SAVI
				load_base_russian_tree = yes
				set_country_flag = make_savinkov_tree_visible
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				country_event = {
					id = rusd.60
					days = 5
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rusd.61
					days = 2
				}
				clr_country_flag = Sergey_L_Markov_dead
				clr_country_flag = Bronislav_V_Kaminski_dead
				clr_country_flag = Vasiliy_V_Biskupskiy_dead
				clr_country_flag = Andrei_A_Vlasov_dead
				clr_country_flag = Nikolay_A_Lokhvitski_dead
				clr_country_flag = Aleksandr_S_Antonov_dead
				clr_country_flag = Vyacheslav_Tkachov_dead
				clr_country_flag = Anton_V_Turkul_dead
				clr_country_flag = Aleksandr_I_Verkhovskiy_dead
				clr_country_flag = Dmitri_N_Verderevsky_dead
				clr_country_flag = Aleksandr_A_Kazakov_dead

setup_sov_cw_victory = {
	hidden_effect = {
		restore_rcw_factories = yes
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = SOV
			}
			SOV = { add_state_core = PREV }
			RUS = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			SOV = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			RVA = { remove_state_core = PREV }
			RVA = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			RRF = { remove_state_core = PREV }
			RRF = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			WRA = { remove_state_core = PREV }
			WRA = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
		}
		SOV = {
			add_stability = 0.15
			load_focus_tree = { tree = Russia_Socialist keep_completed = yes }
		}
	}
}

remove_RCW_claims = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = RUS
					is_claimed_by = RRF
					is_claimed_by = RVA
					is_claimed_by = WRA
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = RRF }
				}
				remove_claim_by = RRF
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = RVA }
				}
				remove_claim_by = RVA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = WRA }
				}
				remove_claim_by = WRA
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = RUS
					is_core_of = RRF
					is_core_of = RVA
					is_core_of = WRA
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = RRF }
				}
				remove_core_of = RRF
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = RVA }
				}
				remove_core_of = RVA
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = WRA }
				}
				remove_core_of = WRA
			}
		}
	}
}
RCW_demobilize_forces = {
	RUS = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Respublikanskoye Opolcheniye" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Respublikanskoye Opolcheniye" disband = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Krasnogvardeitsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Krasnogvardeitsy" disband = yes }
		}
	}
	RRF = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Zelenoarmeitsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Zelenoarmeitsy" disband = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Krasnogvardeitsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Krasnogvardeitsy" disband = yes }
		}
	}
	RVA = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Dobrovoltsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Dobrovoltsy" disband = yes }
		}
	}
	WRA = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Avalovtsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Avalovtsy" disband = yes }
		}
	}
	TRM = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Sibirskiye Dobrovoltsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Sibirskiye Dobrovoltsy" disband = yes }
		}
	}
	LAT = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Krasnogvardeitsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Krasnogvardeitsy" disband = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_template = "Zelenoarmeitsy" }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Zelenoarmeitsy" disband = yes }
		}
	}
}
	
	
create_RCW_militia_template = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = RUS
			RUS = { has_socialist_government = no }
		}
		create_RUS_militia_template = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					tag = RUS
					RUS = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				}
				AND = {
					tag = RRF
					RRF = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				}
				AND = {
					tag = LAT
					LAT = { has_country_flag = LAT_bolsheviks_intervene_in_RCW }
				}
				tag = SOV
			}
		}
		create_SOV_militia_template = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = RRF
			RRF = { has_socialist_government = no }
		}
		create_RRF_militia_template = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = TRM
		}
		create_TRM_militia_template = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = WRA
		}
		create_WRA_militia_template = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = RVA
		}
		create_RVA_militia_template = yes
	}
}
create_RUS_militia_template = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_template = "Respublikanskoye Opolcheniye" }
		}
		division_template = {
			name = "Respublikanskoye Opolcheniye"
			division_names_group = RUS_MIL_01
			regiments = {
				militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
			priority = 0
		}
	}
}

				militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
				militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
			}
			priority = 0
		}
	}
}

RCW_spawn_militia_divisions = {
	### calculate number of units to spawn
	set_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = state_population_k }
	divide_temp_variable = { units_to_spawn = 500 }

	### failsafe so at least one unit is always spawned
	clamp_temp_variable = { var = units_to_spawn min = 1 max = 12 }

	### tooltip
	set_temp_variable = { total_units_to_spawn = units_to_spawn }
	custom_effect_tooltip = RCW_recruit_units

	### spawn normal militias
	set_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { var = units_to_spawn value = 1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		ROOT = { create_RCW_militia_template = yes }
		for_loop_effect = {
			start = 1
			end = units_to_spawn
			compare = less_than_or_equals

			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = [DIVISION] division_template = [TEMPLATE] start_experience_factor = 0.0"
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						owner = ROOT
						id = 1776
					}
				}
				DIVISION = "\\\"[?counter]aya [THIS.GetName] [GetRCWMilitiaName]\\\""
				TEMPLATE = "\\\"[GetRCWMilitiaTemplate]\\\""
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { counter = 1 }
		}
	}
}

RUS_set_zemstvo_result_social = {
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_hospital } #stability
			33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_schools } #pp
			33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_housing } #war support
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
			random_list = {
				50 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_1 }
				50 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_set_zemstvo_result_industry = {
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_civilian_industry } #civilian factories
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_War_Preparations_Programme }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_industry #military factories
			}
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_infrastructure } #infrastructure
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_agriculture } #building slots
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_synthetics  #refinery
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 30
			set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
			random_list = {
				33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_1 }
				33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_2 }
				33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_set_zemstvo_result_research = {
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			30 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research }
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research_bonus }
			30 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_research }
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_research_bonus }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
		}
	}
}

#choosing number of states affected
RUS_pick_zemstvo_states = {
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			RUS_choose_zemstvo_group = yes
			RUS_has_free_building_slots = yes
		}
		save_event_target_as = RUS_zemstvo_state_1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment
				has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				RUS_choose_zemstvo_group = yes
				RUS_has_free_building_slots = yes
				NOT = { state = event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_1 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = RUS_zemstvo_state_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				RUS_choose_zemstvo_group = yes
				RUS_has_free_building_slots = yes
				NOT = {
					state = event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_1
					state = event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_2
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = RUS_zemstvo_state_3
		}
	}
}

RUS_zemstvo_events = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_National_Investment_Bank }
		}
		RUS_zemstvo_focus_events = yes
	}
	else = {
		country_event = rusd.57
	}
}

RUS_zemstvo_focus_events = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Local_Development
				has_completed_focus = RUS_War_Preparations_Programme
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Zemstvo_Research_Initiatives
			}
		}
		country_event = rusd.58
	}
	else = {
		RUS_set_zemstvo_result_social = yes
	}
}

RUS_calculate_zemstva_variables = {
	set_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 25 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 25 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 50 }
	}
}

	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_1
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_2
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_3

	clr_country_flag = RUS_southern_zemstva
	clr_country_flag = RUS_eastern_zemstva
	clr_country_flag = RUS_ural_zemstva

	#bureaucracy
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_schools
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_hospital
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_housing

	#industry
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_civilian_industry
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_industry
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_infrastructure
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_agriculture
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_synthetics

	#research
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research_bonus
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_research
	clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_research_bonus

	#remove ideas
	hidden_effect = {

			RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment
			RUS_large_zemstvo_investment
		}
	}
}

		type = infrastructure
		level = 1

	}

RUS_set_zemstvo_result_social = {
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_hospital } #stability
			33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_schools } #pp
			33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_housing } #war support
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
			random_list = {
				50 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_1 }
				50 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_set_zemstvo_result_industry = {
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_civilian_industry } #civilian factories
			20 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_War_Preparations_Programme }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_industry #military factories
			}
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_infrastructure } #infrastructure
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_agriculture } #building slots
			15 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_synthetics  #refinery
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 30
			set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
			random_list = {
				33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_1 }
				33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_2 }
				33 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure_3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

RUS_set_zemstvo_result_research = {
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			30 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research }
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research_bonus }
			30 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_research }
			20 = { set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_research_bonus }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
		}
	}
}

#choosing number of states affected
RUS_pick_zemstvo_states = {
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			RUS_choose_zemstvo_group = yes
			RUS_has_free_building_slots = yes
		}
		save_event_target_as = RUS_zemstvo_state_1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment
				has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				RUS_choose_zemstvo_group = yes
				RUS_has_free_building_slots = yes
				NOT = { state = event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_1 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = RUS_zemstvo_state_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				RUS_choose_zemstvo_group = yes
				RUS_has_free_building_slots = yes
				NOT = {
					state = event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_1
					state = event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_2
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = RUS_zemstvo_state_3
		}
	}
}

RUS_calculate_expected_monarchy_referendum = {
	set_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_monarchy_popular_support }
	set_temp_variable = { temp2 = RUS_monarchy_candidate_legitimacy }
	set_temp_variable = { temp3 = RUS_monarchy_referendum_legitimacy }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp2 = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { temp3 = 1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp2 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = temp3 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { temp1 = RUS_state_monarchy_referendum_turnout }
	set_variable = { RUS_monarchy_votes_yes = temp1 }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = RUS_monarchy_votes_yes
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
}

initialize_rcw = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_siberia = yes
			is_demilitarized_zone = yes
			is_core_of = SIB
		}
		force_disable_resistance = { clear = yes }
		SIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
		SIB = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rcw.212
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RRF_will_not_spawn }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = yes
				is_core_of = RRF
			}
			RRF = { 
				transfer_state = PREV
				load_oob = "RUS_RRF_civil_war"
			}
		}
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 239
					state = 652
					state = 401
					state = 236
				}
			}
			remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = yes }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 217
					state = 239
					state = 209
					state = 210
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 2 instant_build = yes }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 209
					state = 210
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = { type = industrial_complex level = 2 instant_build = yes }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 258
					state = 223
					state = 222
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = { type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = yes }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:soviet_russia = { exists = yes }
			}

				country_lock_all_division_template = yes
				add_ideas = {
					RCW_major
					extensive_conscription
					war_economy
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = RVA
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RVA
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = RRF
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RRF
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RUS
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = RVA
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RVA
					type = civil_war
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = RRF
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RRF
					type = civil_war
				}
			}

					has_country_flag = RCW_will_declare_war_on_TRM

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RVA
			}
			RVA = { 
				country_lock_all_division_template = yes
				add_ideas = {
					RCW_major
					extensive_conscription
					war_economy
				} 
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:soviet_russia = { exists = yes }
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = event_target:soviet_russia
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = RUS
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = RRF_RVA_ceasefire }
						NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = RRF }
						country_exists = RRF
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RRF
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = RCW_will_declare_war_on_TRM
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = TRM
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = RUS.RUS_starting_states_array
				add_claim_by = RVA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RRF
			}
			RRF = {  
				country_lock_all_division_template = yes
				add_ideas = {
					RCW_major
					extensive_conscription
					war_economy
				}

					limit = {

					}

				if = {

						country_exists = RUS
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

						NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = RVA }
						country_exists = RVA
					}
					declare_war_on = {

					}

						target = TRM
						type = civil_war
					}
				}
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = RUS.RUS_starting_states_array
				add_claim_by = RRF
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = DKB
				DKB = { 
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = RCW_will_intervene
						is_in_faction_with = RVA

					}
				}
			}

					}

					}

					type = civil_war
				}

					target = RRF
					type = civil_war
				}

						is_in_faction_with = RVA
					}
				}

				}

setup_vilnius_accords = {
	set_global_flag = vilnius_accords_active
	# free all puppets 
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of = RUS
		}
		RUS = {
			set_autonomy = { target = PREV autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
		}
	}	
	
	# dissolve the Reichspakt
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				is_subject_of = RUS
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = former_moscow_accord_member
	}
	dismantle_faction = yes

	# give Moscow Accord members military access to each other
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = former_moscow_accord_member
			has_capitulated = no
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = former_moscow_accord_member
				has_capitulated = no
				NOT = { tag = PREV }
			}
			give_military_access = PREV
		}
	}
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = WHR
				tag = LIT
				tag = UKR
				tag = DKB
				tag = KUB
				tag = GEO
				tag = AZE
			}
			exists = no
		}
		release = PREV
		GER = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = ARM
				tag = MTR
			}
			exists = no
		}
		release = PREV
		if = {
			limit = {
				TUR = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			TUR = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			GER = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 12.owner }
	880 = { transfer_state_and_add_core = yes }
	if = {
		limit = {
			FIN = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			FIN = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = FIN_diplomacy } }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = FIN
					is_claimed_by = FIN
					state = 146 #Viipuri
					state = 147 #Kuolajarvi
					state = 213 #Murmansk
					state = 215 #Kem
					state = 216 #Petrozavodsk
					state = 722 #Petsamo
				}
			}
			FIN = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = UKR
				is_claimed_by = UKR
				state = 240
				state = 821
			}
		}
		UKR = { 
			add_state_claim = PREV
			transfer_state = PREV
		}
	}
	every_owned_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = WHR
				is_claimed_by = WHR
				state = 755
				state = 242
				state = 243
				state = 210
			}
		}
		WHR = { 
			add_state_claim = PREV
			transfer_state = PREV
		}
	}
	217 = { add_claim_by = DKB }
		
	save_event_target_as = peace_country
	every_enemy_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = AUS
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
	}
	every_enemy_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = AUS
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
			}
		}
		event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
	}
	every_enemy_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = GER
				is_subject_of = AUS
				is_subject_of = TUR
			}
		}
		event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
	}
	every_enemy_country = {
		limit = {
			is_in_asia = no
		}
		event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
	}
	RUS = {
		country_event = {
			id = rcw.250
			days = 120
		}
	}
}

				tag = GEO
				tag = AZE
				tag = ARM
				tag = DAG
				tag = CRM
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				is_subject_of = TUR
			}
			OR = {
				exists = no
				has_capitulated = yes
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = RUS_OTT_some_concessions
				has_global_flag = RUS_OTT_more_concessions
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = ARM
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = TUR
					is_subject_of = TUR
				}
				OR = {
					exists = no
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		transfer_state = 1213
		add_state_claim = 1213
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
			}
			BUL = { transfer_state = 341 }
		}
		TUR = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = docking_rights
				active = yes
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = docking_rights
					active = yes
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = RUS_OTT_more_concessions
		}
		transfer_state = 1000 #Kars
		add_state_claim = 1000 #Kars
		transfer_state = 1001 #Lazistan
		add_state_claim = 1001 #Lazistan
		if = {
			limit = {
				PER = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = TUR
						is_subject_of = TUR
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 420
			add_state_claim = 420
			transfer_state = 418
			add_state_claim = 418
			transfer_state = 804
			add_state_claim = 804
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
				}
				puppet = PER
			}
		}
	}
	#recheck if OTT is in RSP and kick it
	if = {
		limit = {
			TUR = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
		}
		leave_faction = yes
	}
	save_event_target_as = peace_country
	every_enemy_country = {
		limit = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
	}
	every_enemy_country = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of = TUR
		}
		event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
	}	
}

remove_all_russian_cores = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claimed_by = RUS
				is_core_of = TRM
				is_claimed_by = TRM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = RUS } }
			remove_core_of = RUS
			remove_claim_by = RUS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = TRM } }
			remove_core_of = TRM
			remove_claim_by = TRM
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { country_exists = SIB } }
			remove_core_of = SIB
			remove_claim_by = SIB
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = RUS.RUS_starting_states_array
			add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
		}
	}
}

RUSSIAN_UNIFICATION_play_superevent = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_superevent_trigger_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_I_Bukharin_hog_syn
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Lev Kamenev"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GFX_SPEVNT_RUSSIAN_UNIFICATION_nsp
		hidden_effect = { country_event = super.55 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Maria Spiridonova"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Boris Kamkov"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Isaak Shteinberg"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir Trutovsky"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir Karelin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
